I gave the children a set of children's toiletries, children's bathrobes, and children's slippers. There is no additional charge for the executive lounge. The quality of the lounge happy hour light meals is still good. The variety of food is relatively small, and the biscuits for afternoon tea are particularly delicious. Maybe because there are more guests during the May Day holiday, you need to queue up and wait for a long time for light meals and wine in the evening. The staff is much more enthusiastic than the service of the lobby guy on the first floor (the staff on the first floor basically have no expression on their faces and look indifferent).
The breakfast meets the specifications of a five-star hotel and is quite good.
The water temperature of the swimming pool is suitable and clean. It is no problem for children to go into the water.
The hotel has a small amusement park. Although it is small, it is clean and well-equipped. The children have a lot of fun.
This Marriott in Baiyun is connected by three hotels. It has a Su-style garden building with good scenery. Due to time reasons, I haven't had the opportunity to visit it. The garden is very large and it is very quiet to sleep.
I will stay there next time I travel in the city.

The Lounge is an ideal social space and my favorite part of the hotel.
The indoor green plants and outdoor garden water features give this very business-looking hotel a more resort-like feel.
The Chinese restaurant Man Ho is exquisitely decorated and incorporates many Lingnan elements. It specializes in authentic classic Cantonese cuisine. There is a long corridor here that is quite impressive.
